## 5ï¸âƒ£ Authentication & Authorization

### Ù†Ø¸Ø§Ù… Ø§Ù„Ù…ØµØ§Ø¯Ù‚Ø© (Authentication)

#### ØªØ³Ø¬ÙŠÙ„ Ø§Ù„Ø¯Ø®ÙˆÙ„

```typescript
interface LoginCredentials {
  email: string;
  password: string;
}

interface AuthResponse {
  access_token: string;
  refresh_token?: string;
  user: {
    id: number;
    name: string;
    email: string;
    role: 'super-admin' | 'accountant' | 'store-manager';
    branch?: {
      id: number;
      code: string;
      name: string;
    };
    permissions: string[];
  };
}
```

#### JWT Claims

```json
{
  "sub": 1,
  "name": "Ø£Ø­Ù…Ø¯ Ù…Ø­Ù…Ø¯",
  "email": "ahmed@example.com",
  "role": "store-manager",
  "branch_id": 2,
  "permissions": [
    "voucher.issue.create",
    "voucher.issue.view_own",
    "inventory.view_own",
    "inventory.view_other_branches"
  ],
  "iat": 1697270400,
  "exp": 1697274000
}
```

### Ù†Ø¸Ø§Ù… Ø§Ù„ØªÙÙˆÙŠØ¶ (Authorization)

#### React Context

```typescript
// AuthContext.tsx
interface AuthContextType {
  user: User | null;
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  login: (credentials: LoginCredentials) => Promise<void>;
  logout: () => void;
  hasPermission: (permission: string) => boolean;
  hasRole: (role: string) => boolean;
  canAccessBranch: (branchId: number) => boolean;
}
```

#### Protected Routes

```typescript
// ProtectedRoute.tsx
<Route
  path="/issue-vouchers/create"
  element={
    <ProtectedRoute
      requiredPermission="voucher.issue.create"
      fallback={<Unauthorized />}
    >
      <CreateIssueVoucherPage />
    </ProtectedRoute>
  }
/>
```

#### Permission Guards

```typescript
// usePermission.ts
const { hasPermission, hasRole, canAccessBranch } = useAuth();

// ÙÙŠ Ø§Ù„ÙƒÙˆÙ…Ø¨ÙˆÙ†Ù†Øª
{hasPermission('voucher.issue.approve') && (
  <Button onClick={handleApprove}>Ø§Ø¹ØªÙ…Ø§Ø¯</Button>
)}

{hasRole('super-admin') && (
  <AdminPanel />
)}

{canAccessBranch(branchId) && !hasRole('store-manager') && (
  <EditButton />
)}
```

### Middleware Chain

```typescript
API Request
  â†“
1. JWT Validation
  â†“
2. Extract User & Claims
  â†“
3. Check Role
  â†“
4. Check Permissions
  â†“
5. Check Branch Access (if applicable)
  â†“
6. Allow/Deny
```

### Sprint 7-8: Role-Based Features (Ø£Ø³Ø¨ÙˆØ¹Ø§Ù†)

**Week 7: Permission System**

**Implementation:**
```typescript
// Permission Context
export const PermissionContext = createContext<{
  can: (permission: string) => boolean;
  hasRole: (role: string) => boolean;
  canAccessBranch: (branchId: number) => boolean;
}>({
  can: () => false,
  hasRole: () => false,
  canAccessBranch: () => false,
});

// Hook
export const usePermissions = () => {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  
  return {
    can: (permission: string) => {
      return user?.permissions.includes(permission);
    },
    
    hasRole: (role: string) => {
      return user?.role === role;
    },
    
    canAccessBranch: (branchId: number) => {
      if (user?.role === 'manager') return true;
      if (user?.role === 'accounting') return true; // read-only
      return user?.branch_id === branchId;
    }
  };
};

// Usage in components
const { can, hasRole, canAccessBranch } = usePermissions();

{can('voucher.issue.approve') && (
  <Button onClick={handleApprove}>Ø§Ø¹ØªÙ…Ø§Ø¯</Button>
)}

{canAccessBranch(voucher.branch_id) && !hasRole('accounting') && (
  <Button onClick={handleEdit}>ØªØ¹Ø¯ÙŠÙ„</Button>
)}
```

**Features:**
- âœ… Role-based routing
- âœ… Component-level permissions
- âœ… Branch-based access control
- âœ… Action permissions (view/create/edit/delete/approve)

### Core
- **React 18** - UI library

- **Vite** - Build tool
